***пятьдесят.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятьдесят.html>пятьдеся́т</a> (1202)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compounded from <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a></b> + <b><a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a></b>, or <i>five tens</i>. <b>Десят</b> was the <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span></span> genitive plural, which is required by numbers <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> and up.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятьдесят.html>пятьдеся́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pjatʹdesját</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>fifty (50)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятьдесят.html>пятьдеся́т</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pjatʹdesjat</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nominative case and accusative case governs the genitive plural of the noun. In other cases, it governs the corresponding plural case of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятьдесят.html>пятьдеся́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pjatʹdesját</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>fifty</b> boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятьдесят.html>пятью́десятью</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>pjatʹjúdesjatʹju</b> málʹčikami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with <b>fifty</b> boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пятьдесят.html>пятьдеся́т</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčikov <b>pjatʹdesját</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">approximately <b>fifty</b> boys</span></div></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">полсо́тни</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polsótni</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">used in radio conversations to avoid mixing up with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шестьдесят.html>шестьдеся́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šestʹdesját</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пятидесятиле́тний</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pjatidesjatilétnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся́т</b>
</p><p>Числительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:количественный.html>коли́чественное</a>, соотв. <a href = vnd.unilang:порядковый.html>поря́дковое</a> числительное — <a href = vnd.unilang:пятидесятый.html>пятидеся́тый</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-пять-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-десят-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

</p>

***пятью.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пятью</a> (12122)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пя́тью</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pjátʹju</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>5x, five times as much
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пя́тью</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пя́ть</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пя́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pjátʹju</b> pjátʹ — dvádcatʹ pjátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>five times</b> five is twenty-five</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<div class="NavFrame" style="">

***раб.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раб.html>раб</a> (3238)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">рабъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rabŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbъ</i>. Displaced <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">робъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">robŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раб.html>раб</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rab</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раб.html>раба́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раб.html>рабы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раб.html>рабо́в</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раб.html>раба́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рабыня.html>рабы́ня</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>slave, serf, bondslave <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in common sense and about male person, not female separately</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***работа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́та</a> (133)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:робот.html>ро́бота</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:бот.html>robota</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbòta</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rabota</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence spelling.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rabóta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>work
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́та</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кипеть.html>кипи́т</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Rabóta</b> kipít.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>The work</b> is in full swing.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>labor, toil</li>
<li>assignment, task

***работать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тать</a> (180)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbotati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rabótatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поработать.html>порабо́тать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to work
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> че́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rabótatʹ</b> nad čém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to work on something (must be expressed with an instrumental case)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rabótatʹ</b> na kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to work for someone (must be expressed with an accusative case)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тать</a></b> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rabótatʹ</b> kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to work as [insert occupation or role] (must be expressed with an instrumental case)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тать</a></b> че́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rabótatʹ</b> čém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to work with [insert tool or device] (must be expressed with an instrumental case)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to function</li>
<li>to labor, to toil</li>
<li>to be open <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">for business</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><b>ра<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>бо́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тать.html>тать</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:поработать.html>порабо́тать</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-работ-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>О́бщее</a> прототипическое <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:целенаправленный.html>целенапра́вленно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:действовать.html>де́йствовать</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:изменять.html>изменя́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:материальный.html>материа́льные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:информационный.html>информацио́нные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:объект.html>объе́кты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:создавать.html>создава́я</a> что-либо</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbotьnikъ</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbotьnъ</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ikъ</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:работница.html>рабо́тница</a> (13853)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbotьnica</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbotьnъ</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ica</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работница.html>рабо́тница</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rabótnica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работница.html>рабо́тницы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работница.html>рабо́тницы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работница.html>рабо́тниц</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работник.html>рабо́тник</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>working woman, working girl, female worker</li>
<li>female clerk, female laborer, female employee</li>
<li>maid, housemaid</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работяга.html>работя́га</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rabotjága</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работяга.html>работя́ги</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работяга.html>работя́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работяга.html>работя́г</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> approvingly</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hard worker; plodder, slogger</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:работящий.html>работя́щий</a> (18656)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rabótatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́щий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jáščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; has the form of a present active participle.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работящий.html>работя́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rabotjáščij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> industrious, hardworking</li></ol>

***рабочий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чий</a> (4069)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orboťь</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbota</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-jь</i>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rabóta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rabóčij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чего</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чие</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чих</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чая</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>industrial worker</li>
<li>worker</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rabóčij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>industrial worker's</li>
<li>worker's</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> work, working
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:одежда.html>оде́жда</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rabóčaja</b> odéžda</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>work</b> clothes</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> labor
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́ла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rabóčaja</b> síla</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>man</b>power</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>working, functioning <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of a device, machine, etc.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>; viable, feasible <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of a plan, proposal, etc.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>план</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вроде.html>вро́де</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вполне.html>вполне́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чий</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">étot plan vróde vpolné <b>rabóčij</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this plan seems quite <b>feasible</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>preliminary, working, draft
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:текст.html>те́кста</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rabóčij</b> variánt téksta</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>working</b> version of the text</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рабский.html>ра́бский</a> (14911)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbьskъ</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slave, servant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьskъ</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раб.html>раб</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rab</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> slave; slavish, servile

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рабство.html>ра́бство</a> (8165)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbьstvo</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbъ</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьstvo</i>.

***рабыня.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рабыня.html>рабы́ня</a> (19465)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbyni</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">female slave, maid</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slave, servant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-yni</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рабыня.html>рабы́ня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rabýnja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рабыня.html>рабы́ни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рабыня.html>рабы́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рабыня.html>рабы́нь</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раб.html>раб</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равнина.html>равни́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ravnína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>рав<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ве́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:си.html>си</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-равн-</b>; интерфикс: <b>-о-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-вес-</b>; суффикс: <b>-иj</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-е</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***равнодушие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:равнодушие.html>равноду́шие</a> (6328)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равный.html>ра́вный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rávnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-душа́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-dušá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; literally, "equanimity".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равнодушие.html>равноду́шие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ravnodúšije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равнодушие.html>равноду́шия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равнодушие.html>равноду́шия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равнодушие.html>равноду́ший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>indifference, unconcern, disregard</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>рав<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ду́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ши<span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a |   <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка) |  <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> мн. ч. предположительны <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> неупотребимы.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-равн-</b>; интерфикс: <b>-о-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-душ-</b>; суффикс: <b>-иj</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-е</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><b>рав<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́ш</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равноправный.html>равнопра́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ravnoprávnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)равнопра́внее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)равнопра́вней</b>)

***равный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:равный.html>ра́вный</a> (2099)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">равьнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ravĭnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orvьnъ</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ровный.html>ро́вный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">róvnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равный.html>ра́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rávnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)равне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)равне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>equal (the same in all respects)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одинаковый.html>одина́ковый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odinákovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идентичный.html>иденти́чный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">idɛntíčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совпадать.html>совпада́ющий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sovpadájuščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равноценный.html>равноце́нный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ravnocénnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***равнять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:равнять.html>равня́ть</a> (28374)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равный.html>ра́вный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rávnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равнять.html>равня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ravnjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сравня́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to equalize</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to equate <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равняться.html>равня́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ravnjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сравняться.html>сравня́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to compete, to match
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:никто.html>никто́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:равняться.html>равня́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">niktó ne móžet <b>ravnjátʹsja</b> s nim</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nobody can compete with him, he is without a rival</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be equal, to be equivalent, to amount
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дважды.html>два́жды</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:равняться.html>равня́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шесть.html>шести́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dváždy tri <b>ravnjájetsja</b> šestí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">twice three makes six</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to emulate, to follow the example
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:равняться.html>равня́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лучший.html>лу́чшим</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ravnjátʹsja</b> po lúčšim</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to attain to the level of the best</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dress, to align oneself</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равнять.html>равня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ravnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
